So, the new quantity of oil consumed is:\nNew quantity of oil consumed = Original quantity of oil consumed x (1 - Percentage of reduction)\n= Quantity of oil consumed x (1 - 0.10)\n= 1000 gallons x (1 - 0.10)\n= 900 gallons\nTherefore, the change in the consumer's petroleum bill is:\nChange in petroleum bill = (Original petroleum bill x Percentage of reduction) / 100\n= ($110 x 0.10) / 100\n= $11\nSo, the consumer's petroleum bill would decrease by $11.")

(703, " To estimate the number of infected PCs on the LAN, we can use a proportion based on the sample size and the total number of PCs connected to the LAN.\nLet's start by using the information given in the problem:\n* The administrator has 5.0 minutes to estimate the impact of the virus.\n* The administrator samples 12.0 of the PCs connected to the LAN.\n* 7.0 of the sampled PCs are infected.\nNow, let's convert the sample size and the number of infected PCs in the sample to proportions:\n* Sample size (n): 12.0 = 0.05 x 216.0 (total number of PCs)\n* Number of infected PCs in the sample (n1): 7.0 = 0.03 x 216.0\nNow, we can use the proportion formula to estimate the number of infected PCs on the entire LAN:\nEstimated number of infected PCs = proportion of infected PCs in the sample x total number of PCs\nEstimated number of infected PCs = 0.03 x 216.0 = 6.48\nSo, based on the sample of 12 PCs, it is estimated that approximately 6.5 PCs on the LAN are infected with the virus.")
